     <div>
      <div class="pd-billboard pd-imac-decision-202104 hide as-macbtr-14inch-show as-macbtr-16inch-show" data-analytics-section="decisionsupport">
       <div class="pd-l-plate">
        <div class="pd-billboard-info">
         <h2 class="pd-billboard-header">
          What to consider when choosing your MacBook Pro.
         </h2>
         <p class="pd-billboard-subcopy">
          Configure yours on the next step.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="row">
         <div class="column large-3 small-12">
          <div class="pd-icon-chip">
           <img alt="" class="pd-billboard-hero ir" data-scale-initial="2" data-scale-params-1="wid=36&amp;hei=36&amp;fmt=png-alpha&amp;.v=1633127092000" height="36" src="https://store.storeimages.cdn-apple.com/4982/as-images.apple.com/is/mpb-deciscion-pro-icon-202110?wid=72&amp;hei=72&amp;fmt=png-alpha&amp;.v=1633127092000" width="36"/>
          </div>
          <h3 class="pd-col-title">
           Apple M1 Pro
          </h3>
          <p class="pd-util-compact-right-small-14 hide as-macbtr-14inch-show">
           M1 Pro delivers game-changing performance with amazing battery life. It features up to 10 CPU cores and up to 16 GPU cores, as well as a 16-core Neural Engine and a powerful media engine that can play as many as 4 streams of 8K video.² Delivering 200GB/s of memory bandwidth, M1 Pro can be configured with up to 32GB of unified memory to handle complex professional workflows.
          </p>
          <p class="pd-util-compact-right-small-14 hide as-macbtr-16inch-show">
           M1 Pro delivers game-changing performance with amazing battery life. It features up to 10 CPU cores and up to 16 GPU cores, as well as a 16-core Neural Engine and a powerful media engine that can play as many as 4 streams of 8K video.⁷ Delivering 200GB/s of memory bandwidth, M1 Pro can be configured with up to 32GB of unified memory to handle complex professional workflows.
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="column large-3 small-12">
          <div class="pd-icon-chip">
           <img alt="" class="pd-billboard-hero ir" data-scale-initial="2" data-scale-params-1="wid=36&amp;hei=36&amp;fmt=png-alpha&amp;.v=1633127091000" height="36" src="https://store.storeimages.cdn-apple.com/4982/as-images.apple.com/is/mpb-deciscion-max-icon-202110?wid=72&amp;hei=72&amp;fmt=png-alpha&amp;.v=1633127091000" width="36"/>
          </div>
          <h3 class="pd-col-title">
           Apple M1 Max
          </h3>
          <p class="pd-util-compact-right-small-14 hide as-macbtr-14inch-show">
           When you need the highest level of performance ever in a Mac notebook, there’s M1 Max. It allows you to max out the performance of MacBook Pro with double the GPU core count and memory bandwidth of M1 Pro, and a more powerful media engine that can play up to 5 streams of 8K video.³ You can configure M1 Max with up to 64GB of unified memory, enabling your MacBook Pro to work faster and handle massive files with ease.
          </p>
          <p class="pd-util-compact-right-small-14 hide as-macbtr-16inch-show">
           When you need the highest level of performance ever in a Mac notebook, there’s M1 Max. It allows you to max out the performance of MacBook Pro with double the GPU core count and memory bandwidth of M1 Pro, and a more powerful media engine that can play up to 7 streams of 8K video.⁸ You can configure M1 Max with up to 64GB of unified memory, enabling your MacBook Pro to work faster and handle massive files with ease.
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="column large-3 small-12">
          <div class="pd-icon-memory">
           <img alt="" class="pd-billboard-hero ir" data-scale-initial="2" data-scale-params-1="wid=36&amp;hei=35&amp;fmt=png-alpha&amp;.v=1632803104000" height="35" src="https://store.storeimages.cdn-apple.com/4982/as-images.apple.com/is/mbp-deciscion-memory-icon-202110?wid=72&amp;hei=70&amp;fmt=png-alpha&amp;.v=1632803104000" width="36"/>
          </div>
          <h3 class="pd-col-title">
           Unified Memory
          </h3>
          <p class="pd-util-compact-right-small-14">
           The more unified memory (RAM) you choose, the more apps you can run simultaneously and the better they will perform.
          </p>
          <p class="pd-util-expand-right-large-7 pd-util-compact-right-small-14">
           Unified memory on MacBook Pro allows you to use up to 64GB of memory for graphics tasks — an unprecedented amount for a notebook.
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="column large-3 small-12">
          <div class="pd-icon-thunderbolt">
           <img alt="" class="pd-billboard-hero ir" data-scale-initial="2" data-scale-params-1="wid=36&amp;hei=26&amp;fmt=png-alpha&amp;.v=1632803105000" height="26" src="https://store.storeimages.cdn-apple.com/4982/as-images.apple.com/is/mbp-deciscion-storage-icon-202110?wid=72&amp;hei=52&amp;fmt=png-alpha&amp;.v=1632803105000" width="36"/>
          </div>
          <h3 class="pd-col-title">
           Storage
          </h3>
          <p class="pd-util-compact-right-small-14">
           Solid-state drive (SSD) storage gives you space to store your projects, documents, photos, music, videos, and other files on your MacBook Pro.
          </p>
          <p class="pd-util-compact-right-small-14">
           The SSD in MacBook Pro delivers significant performance and speed that you’ll notice when you start up, launch apps, open project files, and browse your libraries.
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
        <p class="pd-billboard-link">
         Have questions about buying a Mac?
         <a class="as-chat-button active as-buttonlink" data-autom="chat-with-a-specialist-link" data-chat-ui="WEB_CHAT_ACTION_GROUP=DEFAULT;" href="#" target="_blank">
          Chat with a Specialist.
          <span class="a11y">
           (Opens in a new window)
          </span>
         </a>
        </p>
